    \hypertarget{importeren}{%
\section{Importeren}\label{importeren}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Urllib biedt toegang tot html/url's
\item
  BeautifulSoup maakt van rauwe html (lange string) begrijpbare html die
  je kan doorzoeken
\item
  Pymongo is een library om met MongoDB te kunnen connecten
\item
  Datetime is een library die gemakkelijke toegang biedt tot
  datumformaten
\end{itemize}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}1}]:} \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{urllib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{request} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{urlopen}
        \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{bs4} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{BeautifulSoup}
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{pymongo}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}2}]:} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{datetime}
        \PY{n}{now} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{datetime}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{datetime}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{now}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \hypertarget{csv-aanmaken}{%
\section{CSV aanmaken}\label{csv-aanmaken}}

Zoekresultaten kunnen opgeslagen worden in een CSV bestand.
Open(csv-naam, ``w'') --\textgreater{} W staat voor write. Elke aanroep
hiervan maakt het bestand opnieuw aan Kan ook A, dat is zegmaar de A van
Aanvullen.

Niet vergeten het bestand ook te sluiten. DUS: \textgreater{} CSV
openen/aanmaken \textgreater{} CSV schrijven \textgreater{} CSV sluiten 

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}6}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}filenaam = \PYZdq{}huizen.csv\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}header = \PYZdq{}adres, postcode, Woonplaats, prijs, datum, link\PYZbs{}n\PYZdq{}}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f = open(filenaam, \PYZdq{}w\PYZdq{})}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f.write(header)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f.close()}
\end{Verbatim}


    \hypertarget{nieuwehuizenurl}{%
\section{nieuweHuizen(url)}\label{nieuwehuizenurl}}

Functie nieuweHuizen voert, op invoer van een URL, de scraping uit.

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  bs maakt van de html leesbare html
\item
  divje zoekt alle ``a's'' met class-name property-inner en stopt deze
  in een lijst
\item
  van elke divje in de lijst zoeken we het adres, de
  postcode/woonplaats, de prijs, de datum van vinden en de prijs
\item
  deze gegevens tonen we hier in de notebook, én wordt weggeschreven in
  danwel een csv bestand, danwel een noSQL document (mongoDB)
\end{itemize}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{nieuweHuizen}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{url}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{html} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{urlopen}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{url}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{bs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{BeautifulSoup}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{html}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{html.parser}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(bs.a)}
            \PY{n}{divje} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{bs}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findAll}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{a}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{class}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{property\PYZhy{}inner}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
        
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}filenaam = \PYZdq{}huizen.csv\PYZdq{}}
            \PY{n}{tijd} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{now}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strftime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Y }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{B }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{}d}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
            
            \PY{n}{client} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pymongo}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MongoClient}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{db} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{client}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{huis}
           
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f = open(filenaam, \PYZdq{}a\PYZdq{})}
        
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{dif} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{divje}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{adress} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dif}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findAll}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{h2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{class}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{property\PYZhy{}address\PYZhy{}street}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{adres} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{adress}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text}
                \PY{n}{zipWoonplaatss} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dif}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findAll}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{div}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{class}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{property\PYZhy{}address\PYZhy{}zipcity}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{zipWoonplaats} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{zipWoonplaatss}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text} 
                \PY{n}{prijsFind} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dif}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findAll}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{div}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{class}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{property\PYZhy{}price}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{prijs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prijsFind}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text}
                \PY{n}{link} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dif}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{href}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{link}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{adres} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{zipWoonplaats}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{,  }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{prijs} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Gezien op: }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{tijd} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{p}{)}
                \PY{n}{db}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nieuwHuis}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{insert}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{adres}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{adres}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{zipWoonplaats}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{zipWoonplaats}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{prijs}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{prijs}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{tijd}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{tijd}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{link}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{link}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f.write(adres + \PYZdq{}, \PYZdq{} + zipWoonplaats + \PYZdq{}, \PYZdq{} + prijs + \PYZdq{}, \PYZdq{} + tijd + \PYZdq{}, \PYZdq{} + link + \PYZdq{}\PYZbs{}n\PYZdq{})}
                \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(dif)}
        
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}f.close()}
\end{Verbatim}
